defined_text = {
	name = GetCaliphLegitimacyStatus
	random = no

	text = {
		localisation_key = caliph_is_legitimate_successor
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = unified_islam
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = caliph_is_a_puppet
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetCaliphFlag
	random = no
	
	text = {
		localisation_key = "NoCaliph"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_saved_global_event_target = ME_caliphate_tag
					has_saved_global_event_target = Caliph_province
				}
			}
		}
